They instruct you to hold the \\"+\\" button for the 3 seconds to lock and hold the \\"-\\" button for 3 seconds to unlock - TOTALLY WRONG! To lock the buttons you need to hold down the \\"-\\" button for a few seconds, then you'll see a lock symbol appear on the screen, repeat to unlock the buttons and the lock symbol will disappear.   242. Extensive Personal Review (Feel free to gloss over/skip to Final Thoughts/Pros&Cons if Desired) Okay so let me start off by stating the condition of my natural hair. I would describe my hair as having a mixture of fine and medium strands. The growth behind my ears and inner mid section of my head are fine stranded hair. These hairs seem to be the healthiest. Everywhere else seems to be of a medium texture especially the top of my head as it is prone to the most damage. It is also of medium thickness and curly/wavy. I do straighten it weekly so yes I have damage but it is not heavily extensive; just the normal split ends and some weaken strands. Initially I was in search of some kind of anti-frizz serum that would provide me all-day humidity control. This is how I stumbled onto this iron here on Amazon. I have only owned 2 hair straightners in my lifetime. This one here now and an older Remington Wet to Straight Flat iron, which proved to straighten my hair well for years, but after a professional color treatment (something I will never do again), my hair lost much of its natural texture and would no longer hold straight. Minutes after straightening it, I'd step outside and already it'd began frizzing up and becoming poofy. I live in the South so the humidity down here can get pretty bad this time of the year. Growing very tired of constantly restraightening my frizz-prone poofy hair and only further damaging it, I set search for products to help and Amazon brought me here. What struck me and drew me in were all the positive reviews of this product (great frizz-control in humidity and comparisons to the CHI.) I have never owned a CHI, but I figured if it was getting such great reviews and getting comparing it to a \\"high-end iron\\", it'd had to be good, right? And so, I decided to purchase it. (Didn't need that anti-frizz serum after all.) I purchased the iron at a local Walmart, and now regret not purchasing it on here, as it would of saved me some money but all is still good. I'd advise doing some comparative shopping before purchasing to ensure the best price. MY FIRST EXPERIENCE The first time I tried the iron, my hair was already previously straightened using my Remington Wet to Straight Iron, and let me say, my first experience with this iron I did not like so much. I did not find that it straighten my hair as beautifully and flawlessly as some reviews claimed it did. I also really did not like the fact that I could not increase//decrease the temperature in increments of one instead of 10. My first time, I found the temperature of 360 to be too hot, it was frying my ends, and decreasing it brought it down to 340 (a temperaure that at the time I found not hot enough). So there I was with big hopes and expectations and alittle let down. I had plans of returning the very next day, but what stopped me in my tracks was the evident fact that I did find my hair to be less frizzy/poofy outside afterwards. I reasoned the iron had something to do with it, so I decided to give it another go. SECOND TIME Second time using this thing, I decided to wash my hair and allow it to air dry before straightening ( I never blow dry). This time, I saw the difference the reviews were talking about. It did straighten nice and my strands glided through smoothly and effortlessly. There was also a nice sheen and softness to my hair that I had yet to have felt in a long time. My hair actually did feel healthier. I found my perfect temperature too: 340 (very minimal damage to the ends.) This iron does do a very good job of straightening, a much better job than my old Wet to Straight iron. My ends come out straight and soft, almost like when you get a fresh haircut. The old damage is still there and of course still visible, but this thing really camoflauges it while making your hair look and feel so much more softier and healthier. FINAL THOUGHTS I've been owning this iron for about 2 weeks now and I have many reasons to keep it, as well as two reasons to return it, but I find it makes my hair look and feel too beautiful for me to return it! The number one reason why I'd consider returning this iron is the fact that it really gets my hair oily as I am straightening it (has to be the micro conditioning oils.) I do not have naturally oily hair. I straighten my hair at night and fall asleep on it, and this I find is saving me. The fabrics of my bed/pillow must be absorbing a lot of the oils as I sleep, so when I awake I have soft pretty/beautiful hair. :) With the oil though, comes another problem. Now I need to wash my hair more often in between straightenings, which I dislike but do not fear. The oil it produces in the hair, is not a yucky oil, but a soft, smoothing oil. Just find it to be excessive during the straightening process though (feels as if I sprayed my hair with a sheen spray.) If you find that it is also making your hair oily, i'd advice not using any other products in your hair. I find that I don't even need a heat protectant anymore as the oils alone do a very good job of protecting my hair from damage. I did not notice the oily problem the first time (just looked & felt shiny and soft), but up until about 3 uses with the iron, I started to feel it pretty bad (must be a cumulative effect.) Even though the oily-ness can be a bit of a issue for some and myself as well, I still didn't feel the need the knock off 2 stars. The iron nevertheless, is an awesome contender against frizz and humidity. This same oil (oily-ness) is after all what's fighting the frizz.
